				}

		}

		days_remove = 70

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					553 = {
						NOT = {
							any_neighbor_state = {
								CONTROLLER = { OR = { has_war_with = ROOT AND = { tag = ROOT NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } } } }
							}
						}
					}
					554 = {
						NOT = {
							any_neighbor_state = {
								CONTROLLER = { OR = { has_war_with = ROOT AND = { tag = ROOT NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = PREV } } } }
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Ismail Enver Pasa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = enver_power
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { var = enver_power value = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_infl_enver
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Pasa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = cemal_power
					}
					subtract_from_variable = { var = cemal_power value = 1 }

					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_infl_talaat
				}
			}

foreign_politics = {
	TUR_apply_for_a_german_loan_dec = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}

		available = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = WWI_GER_HAS_CAPITULATED
				has_global_flag = WWI_TUR_HAS_CAPITULATED
			}
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = WWI_is_now
			has_focus_tree = Turkey_WWI_focus
			has_country_flag = TUR_can_ask_loan
		}
		
		cost = 10
		days_remove = 35
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = TUR_GER_loan
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = turkey.9 }
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = TUR_GER_loan
				days = 60
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	
	TUR_restore_the_Crimean_Khanate = {
	
		icon = generic_nationalism
	
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = radical_socialism
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = TUR
			has_completed_focus = TUR_compromise_policy
			CRI = {
				is_subject_of = TUR
			}
		}
	
		cost = 15
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 137 } }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			CRI = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				set_cosmetic_tag = CRI_MONARCHY
				add_ideas = CRI_Sultan_Klych-Girey_idea
			}
		}
	}
	
	TUR_restore_the_emirate_of_kuwait = {
	
		icon = generic_nationalism
	
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = radical_socialism
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = TUR
			KUW = { exists = no }
			has_completed_focus = TUR_compromise_policy
			has_completed_focus = TUR_puppet_in_Iran
			has_country_flag = TUR_KUW_is_puppet_WWI
			has_full_control_of_state = 656
		}
	
		cost = 15
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		highlight_states = { highlight_state_targets = { state = 656 } }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = TUR_KUW_is_puppet_WWI
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = KUW	
				}
				remove_claim_by = TUR
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = KUW	
						is_claimed_by = KUW
					}
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				KUW = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			KUW = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				create_country_leader = { name = "Salim Al-Mubarak Al-Sabah" desc = KUW_Salim_Al-Mubarak_Al-Sabah_desc picture = "gfx/leaders/KUW/Portrait_Salim_Al-Mubarak_Al-Sabah.dds" ideology = authoritarism_ideology traits = {  } }
				inherit_technology = TUR
				subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes
			}
		}
	}

	TUR_protectorate_in_the_north_Caucasus = {
	
		icon = generic_nationalism
	
		available = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = radical_socialism
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = TUR
			OR = {
				AND = {
					MRC = {
						exists = no
					}
					any_state = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = MRC
							is_core_of = CIR
							is_core_of = CHC
							is_core_of = DAG
							is_core_of = CBR
							is_core_of = BLK
							is_core_of = OSE
						}
						CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = TUR is_subject_of = TUR is_in_faction_with = TUR } }
					}
				}
				MRC = {
					is_neighbor_of = TUR
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { has_war_with = TUR }
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = TUR_compromise_policy
			has_completed_focus = TUR_holy_war_in_north_caucasus
			has_country_flag = TUR_holy_war_in_north_caucasus_puppet_flag
		}
	
		cost = 15
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = TUR_holy_war_in_north_caucasus_puppet_flag
			if = {
				limit = { MRC = { exists = no } }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = MRC
							is_core_of = CIR
							is_core_of = CHC
							is_core_of = DAG
							is_core_of = CBR
							is_core_of = BLK
							is_core_of = OSE
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = TUR
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = MRC
							is_core_of = CIR
							is_core_of = CHC
							is_core_of = DAG
							is_core_of = CBR
							is_core_of = BLK
							is_core_of = OSE
						}
						NOT = { is_core_of = MRC }
					}
					add_core_of = MRC
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = MRC
						is_controlled_by = TUR
					}
					MRC = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				MRC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = despotism
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					set_cosmetic_tag = MRC_MONARCHY
					inherit_technology = TUR
					subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_semi_independent = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				MRC = {
					country_event = turkey.34
				}
			}
		}
	}

							tag = GEO

							tag = AZR
							tag = BAK

					}
					NOT = {

							state = 352
							state = 353
							state = 354
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = TUR_GEO_peace_delay
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			GEO = { country_event = { id = rcw_tc.38 days = 1 } }
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = TUR_GEO_peace_delay
				days = 60
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}

					has_government = communism
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = TUR
			has_country_flag = TUR_pan_turanist_propaganda_enable
			1073 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = pan_turanist_agitation }
				compliance > 89
				resistance < 10
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}

			factor = 100
		}

			1073 = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = pan_turanist_agitation }

					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = pan_islamic_agitation }
				}

					remove_claim_by = TUR

			}

TUR_young_turkish_triumvirate_decisions = {
	TUR_triumvirate_reduce_tension = {
	
		icon = generic_political_discourse
	
		available = {
			has_government = despotism
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = TUR
			OR = {
				has_variable = enver_power
				has_variable = cemal_power
				has_variable = talaat_power
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = enver_power
					check_variable = {
						var = enver_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					set_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = enver_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = 2 }
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = temp_enver_power
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = talaat_power
						value = temp_enver_power
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = cemal_power
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					set_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = cemal_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = 2 }
					check_variable = {
						var = talaat_power
						value = temp_cemal_power
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = talaat_power
					check_variable = {
						var = talaat_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					set_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = talaat_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = 2 }
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = temp_talaat_power
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		cost = 25
		
		days_remove = 20
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.03
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = enver_power
					check_variable = {
						var = enver_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { var = enver_power value = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_infl_enver
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = cemal_power
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { var = cemal_power value = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_infl_cemal
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_variable = talaat_power
					check_variable = {
						var = talaat_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { var = talaat_power value = 1 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_infl_talaat
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {}
	}

	TUR_cemal_intrigues = {
	
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { has_variable = cemal_power }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		
		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
			has_variable = cemal_power
		}
		
		is_good = no
		
		priority = 10
		
		days_mission_timeout = 40
		
		timeout_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					add_to_variable = { var = cemal_power value = 1 }
					custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_infl_cemal
				}
				50 = {}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = 5
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = { cemal_power < 7 }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = {}
					30 = { country_event = turkey.69 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = cemal_power
						value = 7
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					50 = {}
					50 = { country_event = turkey.69 }
				}
			}
			activate_mission = TUR_cemal_intrigues
		}
	}
	
	TUR_cemal_intrigues_coup = {
	
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { has_variable = cemal_power }
				has_country_flag = TUR_cemal_talaat_is_ally
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		
		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
			has_variable = cemal_power
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_cemal_talaat_is_ally }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_cemal_angry
				AND = {
					has_variable = civil_power
					has_variable = military_power
					set_temp_variable = { temp_civil_power = civil_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_civil_power = 2 }
					check_variable = {
						var = military_power
						value = temp_civil_power
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_variable = enver_power
					has_variable = talaat_power
					OR = {
						AND = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
							has_variable = enver_power
							set_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = enver_power }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = 3 }
							check_variable = {
								var = cemal_power
								value = temp_enver_power
								compare = less_than
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
							has_variable = enver_power
							set_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = cemal_power }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = 3 }
							check_variable = {
								var = cemal_power
								value = temp_cemal_power
								compare = less_than
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
							has_variable = talaat_power
							set_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = talaat_power }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = 3 }
							check_variable = {
								var = cemal_power
								value = temp_enver_power
								compare = less_than
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
							has_variable = talaat_power
							set_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = cemal_power }
							subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = 3 }
							check_variable = {
								var = talaat_power
								value = temp_cemal_power
								compare = less_than
							}
						}
					}
				}
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = enver_power
						set_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = enver_power }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = 2 }
						check_variable = {
							var = cemal_power
							value = temp_enver_power
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = enver_power
						set_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = cemal_power }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = 2 }
						check_variable = {
							var = cemal_power
							value = temp_cemal_power
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = talaat_power
						set_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = talaat_power }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_talaat_power = 2 }
						check_variable = {
							var = cemal_power
							value = temp_enver_power
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
						has_variable = talaat_power
						set_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = cemal_power }
						subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_cemal_power = 2 }
						check_variable = {
							var = talaat_power
							value = temp_cemal_power
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		is_good = no
		
		priority = 10
		
		days_mission_timeout = 100
		
		timeout_effect = {
			
		}
	}
	
	TUR_talaat_intrigues = {
	
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { has_variable = talaat_power }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		
		activation = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
			has_variable = talaat_power
		}
		
		is_good = no
		
		priority = 10
		
		days_mission_timeout = 40
		
		timeout_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					random_list = {
						70 = {
							add_to_variable = { var = talaat_power value = 1 }
							custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_infl_talaat
						}
						30 = {
							add_to_variable = { var = talaat_power value = 2 }
							custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_infl_talaat_2
						}
					}
				}
				50 = {}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { talaat_power > 7 }
				}
				random_list = {
					70 = {}
					30 = { country_event = turkey.69 }
				}
			}
			activate_mission = TUR_talaat_intrigues
		}
	}
	
	TUR_talaat_intrigues_coup = {

		}

	TUR_twice_intrigues_coup = {
	
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				has_country_leader = { name = "Ahmet Cemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				NOT = { has_variable = enver_power }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_cemal_talaat_is_ally }
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
		}
		
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_cemal_talaat_is_ally
			has_variable = enver_power
			has_variable = cemal_power
			has_variable = talaat_power
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = enver_power
					set_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = cemal_power }
					add_to_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = talaat_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = 3 }
					check_variable = {
						var = enver_power
						value = temp_duumvirate_power
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = enver_power
					set_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = cemal_power }
					add_to_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = talaat_power }
					subtract_from_temp_variable = { temp_duumvirate_power = 2 }
					check_variable = {
						var = enver_power
						value = temp_duumvirate_power
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 100
		
		timeout_effect = {
			
		}

	TUR_antiwar_coup = {
	
		allowed = {
			tag = TUR
		}
		
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Mustafa Kemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_weak_control_WWI }
					#NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Otto Liman von Sanders" ruling_only = yes } }
					has_stability > 0.19
					surrender_progress < 0.4
				}
				any_unit_leader = { NOT = { OR = { has_id = 77408 has_id = 90005 } } }
			}
		}
		
		available = {
			has_country_leader = { name = "Mustafa Kemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
		}
		
		activation = {
			has_global_flag = WWI_is_now
			NOT = { has_global_flag = WWI_TUR_HAS_CAPITULATED }
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mustafa Kemal Paşa" ruling_only = yes } }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_weak_control_WWI
				#has_country_leader = { name = "Otto Liman von Sanders" ruling_only = yes }
				has_stability < 0.2
				surrender_progress > 0.39

		}

	TUR_triumvirate_remove_cemal = {
	
		icon = generic_political_discourse
	
		available = {
			has_government = despotism
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = enver_power
					check_variable = {
						var = enver_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
					has_variable = talaat_power
					check_variable = {
						var = talaat_power
						value = 3
						compare = greater_than_or_equals

			}
		}

			factor = 0
		}

			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_triumvirate_remove_effect
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_is_under_control_GER } }
					if = {

							OR = {

										value = enver_power
										compare = greater_than_or_equals
									}
								}
								AND = {
									has_country_leader = { name = "Mehmed Talaat Paşa" ruling_only = yes }

										compare = greater_than_or_equals
									}
								}
							}
						}
						random_list = {
							50 = { country_event = turkey.74 }
							50 = { country_event = turkey.75 }
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								AND = {
									has_country_leader = { name = "İsmail Enver Paşa" ruling_only = yes }
									has_variable = enver_power
									set_temp_variable = { temp_enver_power = enver_power }

									}
								}

									}
								}
							}
						}
